# %W% %T% %D%  
# DESCRIPTION-- Daily backup schedule for lawson.
# DEPENDENCIES--
# CREATED -- 05/04/00 by J. Norris

SCHEDULE AMFINAN1#OBDLYLAW 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY"
AT 2000 
CARRYFORWARD
:
AMFINAN1#BSTOPLL

# FOLLOWS JDAPROD#JLOADLAW.@

ORAPRDP#BCTRLDLO
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL

ORAPRDP#BSTPDLO
 FOLLOWS BCTRLDLO
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL

#********* Create snapshots **********

AMFINAN1#BSNCRLPA
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL

ORAPRDP#BSNCROPA
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

ORAPRDP#BSNCROPO
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

#********* Create Commvault Snapshots **********

AMFINAN1#COMMVAULT_START
 FOLLOWS BSNCRLPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPO
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

ORAPRDP#COMMVAULTO
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPO
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

AMFINAN1#COMMVAULTL
 FOLLOWS BSNCRLPA
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

AMFINAN1#COMMVAULT_END
 FOLLOWS COMMVAULTL
 FOLLOWS COMMVAULTO

#********* Vault snapshots **********

AMFINAN1#VAULT
 FOLLOWS BSNCRLPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPO
 FOLLOWS COMMVAULTL
 FOLLOWS COMMVAULTO

#********* Start Lawson **********

ORAPRDP#BSTRDLO
 AT 2015 
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPO
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

AMFINAN1#BSTRTLL
 FOLLOWS BSNCRLPA
 FOLLOWS BSTRDLO
 FOLLOWS AMFINAN1#UTDELJOBHST.LAWLOGPRG 

#********* Delete snapshots **********

AMFINAN1#DELETE_SNAPS_PRI

AMFINAN1#DELETE_SNAPS_BKUP
END

# DESCRIPTION-- Analyze current partition of JDA objects

# CREATED -- 11/14/11 by D. Wesolowski

ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY;"
AT 1900 
CARRYFORWARD
FOLLOWS JDADEV#BACKUP_JDA.START_JDAP 
:
JDADEV#ANAPART1

JDADEV#ANAPART2
 FOLLOWS JDADEV#JMAIN.JDAPMM_UPLOAD_6 
END

# %W% %T% %D%  
# DESCRIPTION--
# DEPENDENCIES--
# CREATED --  by M. Vogt
# ALTERED -- 

SCHEDULE JDADEV#ANALZYEPART 
ON REQUEST
:
JDADEV#ANAPART2
END

# Version: %I%
# Date:    %D%
# Time:    %T%
#
# DESCRIPTION-- JDAP database break.  Takes backup of jda volumes and controls access to JDA PMM.

SCHEDULE JDADEV#BACKUP_JDA 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY"
AT 1900 
CARRYFORWARD
:
JDADEV#SHUTDOWN_JDAP

JDADEV#DELETE_PRI_JDA

JDADEV#DELETE_BKUP_JDA
 FOLLOWS DELETE_PRI_JDA

JDADEV#SNAP_JDA
 FOLLOWS SHUTDOWN_JDAP

JDADEV#SNAP_APPS
 FOLLOWS SNAP_JDA

JDADEV#COMMVAULT_START
 FOLLOWS SNAP_APPS
 FOLLOWS SNAP_JDA

JDADEV#COMMVAULT
 FOLLOWS SNAP_APPS
 FOLLOWS SNAP_JDA

JDADEV#COMMVAULT_END
 FOLLOWS COMMVAULT

JDADEV#VAULT_JDA
 FOLLOWS SNAP_APPS
 FOLLOWS SNAP_JDA

JDADEV#START_JDAP
 AT 1915 
 FOLLOWS SNAP_APPS
 FOLLOWS SNAP_JDA
END

#$SCHEDULES
# 
#         NAME: twsdef_ju_move_ssh_4.she
#  DESCRIPTION: UTILITY - Move files between SSH accounts
#                         The JDA server serves as a sftp host for sharing data with BATO.
#                         It serves the same role for FNA, Lawson and HeMS.
#                         When BSRO systems other than JDA need to share data with SAP
#                         they drop into their SSH folder on JDA and this utility moves
#                         it into the BATO folder and visa-versa.
#
# DEPENDENCIES: None
#
# Runs Daily at 0330

#         NAME: twsdef_jnawave.she
#  DESCRIPTION: Load NA billing file into JDA
#               Loads POS sales data
#               Processes Outside Purchase and Inventory adj
# DEPENDENCIES: JANALYZED.@
#               JSQLTEST.@
#               JMAIN.JTRAN1SA
#
#               NOTE* JDASTAMP   defined in twsdef_jda_common.job
#                     JDRTLD02   defined in twsdef_jda_common.job
#                     JDRTLD01   defined in twsdef_jda_common.job
#                     J230A1IA   defined in twsdef_jda_common.job
#                     J230A_MVSA defined in twsdef_jda_common.job
#                     J225A1IA   defined in twsdef_jda_common.job
#                     J225A1MU   defined in twsdef_jda_common.job
#                     J225A1MA   defined in twsdef_jda_common.job
#
# Runs MO,TU,WE,TH,FR,SA at 2000
#
# HISTORY
#   $Log[10]:
#    6    TWS        1.5         4/22/16 12:14:43 PM CDTRuss Lupo       another
#          try at the input directory
#         
#    5    TWS        1.4         4/22/16 12:11:09 PM CDTRuss Lupo       once
#         again changed the place to look for files from NA
#         
#    4    TWS        1.3         4/22/16 11:53:16 AM CDTRuss Lupo       another
#          try at OPENS
#         
#    3    TWS        1.2         4/22/16 11:28:50 AM CDTRuss Lupo       fixed
#         OPENS directory
#         
#    2    TWS        1.1         4/21/16 2:35:55 PM CDT Phil Speer      AIX JDA
#          Upgrade
#         
#    1    TWS        1.0         4/12/16 4:12:11 PM CDT Phil Speer      initial
#          revision
#   $
#
#############################
#@(#)$Header: twsdef_jnawave.she, 6, 4/22/16 12:14:43 PM CDT, Russ Lupo$

SCHEDULE JDAQA#JNAWAVE 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=WEEKLY;BYDAY=MO,TU,WE,TH,FR,SA"
AT 2000 
CARRYFORWARD
FOLLOWS JDAQA#JANALYZD.@ 
FOLLOWS JDAQA#JSQLTEST.@ 
FOLLOWS JDAQA#JMAIN.JTRAN1SA 
:
JDAQA#JDASTAMP

JDAQA#JNAFILCK
OPENS JDAQA#"^JDBASDIR^/input/jda418a.out.*"
 FOLLOWS JDASTAMP

JDAQA#JNAFILDC
 FOLLOWS JNAFILCK

JDAQA#JNAFILRC
 FOLLOWS JNAFILCK

JDAQA#JNAFILSF
 FOLLOWS JNAFILRC

JDAQA#J418A1LA
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDROUTER
 FOLLOWS JNAFILSF

JDAQA#J418A1MA
 FOLLOWS J418A1LA

JDAQA#JNAFILRM
 FOLLOWS J418A1MA

JDAQA#JNAARCRENTAL2
 FOLLOWS JNAFILRM

JDAQA#JNAARCRENTAL3
 FOLLOWS JNAARCRENTAL2

JDAQA#JNAARCRENTAL4
 FOLLOWS JNAARCRENTAL3

JDAQA#JDLRTIRE
 FOLLOWS JNAARCRENTAL4

JDAQA#JDRTLD02
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDROUTER
 FOLLOWS JDASTAMP

JDAQA#JDRTLD01
 AT 2015 
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDROUTER
 FOLLOWS JDASTAMP
 FOLLOWS JDRTLD02

JDAQA#JNAWAVECK
 FOLLOWS JDRTLD01

JDAQA#J230A1IA
NEEDS 1 AMFINAN1#LNAPDAPS
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDROUTER
 FOLLOWS JNAWAVECK
 FOLLOWS JDAQA#JMAIN.JITEM1SA 

JDAQA#J230A_MVSA
 FOLLOWS J230A1IA

JDAQA#J225A1IA
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDROUTER
 FOLLOWS JDRTLD01

JDAQA#J225A1MU
 FOLLOWS J225A1IA

JDAQA#J225A1MA
 FOLLOWS J225A1MU

JDAQA#JDAPMM_UPLOAD_1
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#J9INLOCK
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#UPLOAD
 FOLLOWS J225A1MA
 FOLLOWS J230A_MVSA

JDAQA#JNACNLXA
 AT 2100 

JDAQA#JNACNLDJ
 FOLLOWS JNACNLXA
END

#$SCHEDULES
# 
#         NAME: twsdef_jreplenishment.she
#  DESCRIPTION: Replenishment and reports
# DEPENDENCIES: JMAIN.JEODA1SA (JDA EOD from Previous Day))
#
#               
#
# Runs Daily at 0600
#
# HISTORY
#   $Log[10]:
#    16   TWS        1.15        10/6/17 9:41:01 AM CDT Sandeep Balan   added
#         UPLOAD resource for job step JDAPMM_PMGHDRCRE
#         
#    15   TWS        1.14        9/28/16 1:53:20 PM CDT Phil Speer
#         JDARPT_REPL_ALERT will execute every hour until canceled
#         
#    14   TWS        1.13        9/28/16 12:49:31 PM CDTPhil Speer
#         JDARPT_REPL_ALERT_ABEND not excutes at 0805
#         
#    13   TWS        1.12        9/8/16 5:04:17 PM CDT  Phil Speer      Done
#         alert follows repl report / only repl job step depends on
#         main.jeoda1sa
#         
#    12   TWS        1.11        7/20/16 11:25:01 AM CDTPhil Speer      Added
#         +1 DAYS to jobstep JDARPT_REPL_ALERT, JDARPT_REPL_ALERT_ABEND
#         
#    11   TWS        1.10        7/13/16 1:05:15 PM CDT Siva Nelluri    Removed
#          dependency on ji_trfprm_jd_trf. This need to be added back once
#         transfer parameters work items is ready. 
#    10   TWS        1.9         7/1/16 3:20:28 PM CDT  Siva Nelluri    Added
#         new jobs for alert notifications and abend
#         
#    9    TWS        1.8         6/24/16 4:13:18 PM CDT Phil Speer      Added
#         ji_trfprm_jd_trf depedency
#         
#    8    TWS        1.7         6/13/16 12:55:56 PM CDTPhil Speer      Added
#         time dependency AT 0100
#         
#    7    TWS        1.6         6/6/16 12:55:51 PM CDT Doug Buss       Removed
#          previous and timeframe from the schedule
#         
#   $
#
#############################
#@(#)$Header: twsdef_jreplenishment.she, 16, 10/6/17 9:41:01 AM CDT, Sandeep Balan$

SCHEDULE JDAQA#JREPLENISHMENT 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY;"
AT 0100 
CARRYFORWARD
:
JDAQA#JDAPMM_REPL
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDAREPL
 FOLLOWS JDAQA#JMAIN.JEODA1SA 

JDAQA#JDARPT_REPLEN_REPORT
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDAREPL
 FOLLOWS JDAPMM_REPL

JDAQA#JDAPMM_TRFREQREL
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDAREPL
 FOLLOWS JDARPT_REPLEN_REPORT

JDAQA#JDAPMM_TRFBAPUO
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDAREPL
 FOLLOWS JDAPMM_TRFREQREL

JDAQA#JDAPMM_PMGHDRCRE
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#JDAREPL
NEEDS 1 JDAQA#UPLOAD
 FOLLOWS JDAPMM_TRFBAPUO

JDAQA#JDARPT_REPL_ALERT_DONE
 FOLLOWS JDARPT_REPLEN_REPORT

JDAQA#JDARPT_REPL_ALERT
 AT 0600 +1 DAYS 
 EVERY 0100

JDAQA#JDARPT_REPL_ALERT_ABEND
 AT 0805 +1 DAYS 
END

#         NAME: def_ju_move_ssh_1.she
#  DESCRIPTION: UTILITY - Move files between SSH accounts
#                         The JDA server serves as a sftp host for sharing data with BATO.
#                         It serves the same role for FNA, Lawson and HeMS.
#                         When BSRO systems other than JDA need to share data with SAP
#                         they drop into their SSH folder on JDA and this utility moves
#                         it into the BATO folder and visa-versa.
#
# DEPENDENCIES: None
#
# Runs Daily at 1400
#
# HISTORY
#   $Log[10]:
#    1    TWS        1.0         3/16/16 4:45:12 PM CDT Phil Speer      initial
#          revision
#   $
#
#############################

ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY;"
AT 1400 
CARRYFORWARD
:
JDAQA#JDAUTL_MOVE_SSH_FILES
END

# @(#)OBDLYNAS.she	1.5 11:12:18 11/01/26  
# DESCRIPTION-- Daily backup schedule for nasrv.
# DEPENDENCIES--
# CREATED -- 05/16/05 by J. Norris

SCHEDULE NASRV#OBDLYNAS 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=WEEKLY;BYDAY=SU,MO,TU,WE,TH,FR"
AT 1930 
CARRYFORWARD
:
NASRV#SNAPSTAMP1

N4ABLAST#SNAPSTAMP2

#********* Rename snapshots and stop DB **********
# FOLLOWS NASRV#NA_DLY_M_SA.EH_DELETES 

NASRV#BSNRENA3
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP1
 FOLLOWS NASRV#OBDLYNAS.BSNDINA3 PREVIOUS

# FOLLOWS NASRV#OBWKYNAS.BSNDINA3 PREVIOUS
# FOLLOWS NASRV#NA_DLY_M_SA.EH_DELETES 

NASRV#BSNRENAA
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP1
 FOLLOWS NASRV#OBDLYNAS.BSNDINAA PREVIOUS

# FOLLOWS NASRV#OBWKYNAS.BSNDINAA PREVIOUS

NASRV#NADCAPST

# FOLLOWS NASRV#NA_DLY_M_SA.EH_DELETES 

NASRV#NADBLOCK
 FOLLOWS BSNRENA3
 FOLLOWS BSNRENAA
 FOLLOWS NADCAPST

#********* Create snapshots and start DB **********

NASRV#BSNCRNA3
 FOLLOWS BSNRENA3
 FOLLOWS NADBLOCK
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP1

NASRV#BSNCRNAA
 FOLLOWS BSNRENAA
 FOLLOWS NADBLOCK
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP1

NASRV#NADUBLCK
 FOLLOWS BSNCRNA3
 FOLLOWS BSNCRNAA
 FOLLOWS NADBLOCK

NASRV#NADBCOPY
 FOLLOWS NADUBLCK

#********* Connect nasrv snapshots **********

N4ABLAST#BSNCONA3
 AT 2130 
NEEDS 1 N4ABLAST#LVMTAB
 FOLLOWS BSNCRNA3
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP2

N4ABLAST#BSNCONAA
 AT 2130 
NEEDS 1 N4ABLAST#LVMTAB
 FOLLOWS BSNCRNAA
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP2

#********* Initiate nasrv Backups **********

N4ABLAST#NBUDLNAS
 FOLLOWS BSNCONA3
 FOLLOWS BSNCONAA

N4ABLAST#BBUDLNAS
NEEDS 1 N4ABLAST#NETBAKUP
OPENS N4ABLAST#"/netbackup/var/nb.lock"
 FOLLOWS BSNCONA3
 FOLLOWS BSNCONAA

N4ABLAST#NBUDLNAAN
 FOLLOWS BSNCONAA

N4ABLAST#BBUDLNAAN
NEEDS 1 N4ABLAST#NETBAKUP
OPENS N4ABLAST#"/netbackup/var/nb.lock"
 FOLLOWS BSNCONAA

N4ABLAST#NBUDLNAIN
 FOLLOWS BSNCONA3

N4ABLAST#BBUDLNAIN
NEEDS 1 N4ABLAST#NETBAKUP
OPENS N4ABLAST#"/netbackup/var/nb.lock"
 FOLLOWS BSNCONA3

#********* Disconnect nasrv snapshots **********

N4ABLAST#BSNDINA3
NEEDS 1 N4ABLAST#LVMTAB
 FOLLOWS BBUDLNAIN
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP2

N4ABLAST#BSNDINAA
NEEDS 1 N4ABLAST#LVMTAB
 FOLLOWS BBUDLNAAN
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP2

#********* Delete snapshots **********

NASRV#BSNDENA3
 AT 0800 +1 DAYS 
 FOLLOWS BSNRENA3
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP1

NASRV#BSNDENAA
 AT 0800 +1 DAYS 
 FOLLOWS BSNRENAA
 FOLLOWS SNAPSTAMP1

NASRV#RMSTAMP1
 FOLLOWS BSNCRNA3
 FOLLOWS BSNCRNAA
 FOLLOWS BSNDENA3
 FOLLOWS BSNDENAA
 FOLLOWS BSNRENA3
 FOLLOWS BSNRENAA

N4ABLAST#RMSTAMP2
 FOLLOWS BSNCONA3
 FOLLOWS BSNCONAA
 FOLLOWS BSNDINA3
 FOLLOWS BSNDINAA
END

# %W% %T% %D%  
# DESCRIPTION-- Daily snapshot database schedule for oraprod.
# DEPENDENCIES--
# CREATED -- 07/13/11 by J. Norris

SCHEDULE TWSDEV#C901 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY;"
AT 2300 
CARRYFORWARD
:
#********* Stop database **********

ORAPRDP#STOPC901
 PRIORITY 80

#********* Disconnect snapshot **********

ORAPRDP#EXPORTC901CLONE
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS STOPC901

#********* Disconnect snapshot **********

ORAPRDP#DELETEC901CLONE
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS EXPORTC901CLONE

#********* Store weekday **********

ORAPRDP#C901SNAPDAY
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS DELETEC901CLONE

#********* Connect snapshot **********

ORAPRDP#CREATEC901CLONE
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS C901SNAPDAY

#********* Connect snapshot **********

ORAPRDP#IMPORTC901CLONE
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS CREATEC901CLONE

#********* Chown oracle **********

ORAPRDP#CHOWNORA
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS IMPORTC901CLONE

#********* Start database **********

ORAPRDP#STARTC901
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS CHOWNORA
END

# @(#)C901HIST.she	1.3 15:42:58 16/01/25  
# DESCRIPTION-- Refresh C901 snapshot.  Please read instructions
# DEPENDENCIES--
# CREATED -- 06/27/2019 Ryan Kovacik
# 
# Instructions:
# If refreshing yesterday's data, just run this as-is.  The /OBSNDBLA
#     file on Oradev will automatically still have the date stamp
#     from when it was last run.
# You can refresh data that existed up to 35 days ago.  In order to
#     load the checkpoint's data from a particur day
#     1) Log into ORADEV
#     2) Change the date written in the file /OBSNDBLA to the day you
#        need to refresh.  MMDDYYYY format
#     3) Save the file
#     4) Run this C901HIST schedule

SCHEDULE TWSDEV#C901HIST 
ON REQUEST
CARRYFORWARD
:
#********* Stop database **********

ORAPRDP#STOPC901HIST
 PRIORITY 80

#********* Disconnect snapshot **********

ORAPRDP#EXPORTC901CLONEHIST
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS STOPC901HIST

#********* Disconnect snapshot **********

ORAPRDP#DELETEC901CLONEHIST
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS EXPORTC901CLONEHIST

#********* Connect snapshot **********

ORAPRDP#CREATEC901CLONEHIST
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS DELETEC901CLONEHIST

#********* Connect snapshot **********

ORAPRDP#IMPORTC901CLONEHIST
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS CREATEC901CLONEHIST

#********* Set volume priorities **********

ORAPRDP#DOTPATHSHIST
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS IMPORTC901CLONEHIST

#********* Chown oracle **********

ORAPRDP#CHOWNORAHIST
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS DOTPATHSHIST

#********* Start database **********

ORAPRDP#STARTC901HIST
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS CHOWNORAHIST
END

SCHEDULE TWSDEV#CTDWQA 
ON RUNCYCLE WEEKLY "FREQ=WEEKLY;BYDAY=SA,SU"
AT 2020 
CARRYFORWARD
NEEDS 1 HEMSQA#HQACLONE
:
HEMSQA#TDWQA_SNAPDAY
 PRIORITY 80

HEMSQA#STOP_TDWQA
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS TDWQA_SNAPDAY

HEMSQA#EXPORT_TDWQA
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS STOP_TDWQA

HEMSQA#DELETE_TDWQA
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS EXPORT_TDWQA

HEMSQA#CREATE_TDWQA
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS DELETE_TDWQA

HEMSQA#IMPORT_TDWQA
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS CREATE_TDWQA

HEMSQA#START_TDWQA
 PRIORITY 80
 FOLLOWS IMPORT_TDWQA
END

#@(#) $Id: Sfinal.conf,v 7.56 1995/02/24 04:13:53 alanh viola_thunder $
#  This is a sample schedule for doing pre and post production
#  processing.  It assumes the start time is 6:00 a.m.
#
#  It is defined as CARRYFORWARD because it is executed across
#  production days.  This ensures that job statistics will be
#  collected for the schedule.
#
#  All of the job statements that follow use auto-documentation
#  keywords so the jobs will be documented by composer when the
#  schedule is added or modified in the mastsked file.

SCHEDULE TWSDEV#FINAL 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY;"
AT 0559 
CARRYFORWARD
FOLLOWS TWSDEV#FINAL.@ PREVIOUS
:
TWSDEV#STARTAPPSERVER

TWSDEV#MAKEPLAN
 FOLLOWS STARTAPPSERVER

TWSDEV#SWITCHPLAN
 FOLLOWS MAKEPLAN

TWSDEV#CREATEPOSTREPORTS
 FOLLOWS SWITCHPLAN

#  MakePlan creates tomorrow's production control file (Symnew). 
#  Then it runs reporter to print  pre-production reports.
#  The reports should be reviewed.
#  SwitchPlan stops batchman and runs stageman to: 1) carry forward incomplete schedules,
#  2) log the old Symphony file, 3) create the new Symphony and Sinfonia
#  files.  It then starts batchman.
#  CreatePostReports runs reporter to print post-production reports.
#  UpdateStats runs logman to log job statistics, and then
#  report8 to print the Job Histogram.

TWSDEV#UPDATESTATS
 FOLLOWS SWITCHPLAN
END

END

:
END

ON RUNCYCLE BENOW2 VALIDFROM 07/09/2013 02/28/2014
ON RUNCYCLE BIWEEKLY "FREQ=WEEKLY;INTERVAL=2;BYDAY=SU"
ON RUNCYCLE RC1 "FREQ=MONTHLY;INTERVAL=1;BYMONTHDAY=-2"
:
END
